ACTOR AyaDecorationScripted 31334
{
//$Category "Touhou Decor"
  Scale 0.7
  Game Doom
  Radius 24
  Height 64
  +SOLID
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    SHMI ABCDEFGH 3
	Loop
  BlowUp:
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/defeat",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 BRIGHT A_SpawnItemEx("TouhouFireWhite",frandom(4,-4),frandom(4,-4),frandom(4,-4),frandom(8,-8),frandom(8,-8),frandom(8,-8),frandom(0,360),0,0)
	Stop
  }
}

ACTOR Reimu 31311
{
//$Category "Touhou Characters"
  Tag "Reimu Hakurei"
  Speed 12
  MONSTER
  Health 2500
  Radius 20
  Height 62
  Scale 0.7
  Mass 1000000
  MeleeThreshold 64
  MeleeRange 64
  Damage 0
  DamageFactor "ReimuDamage", 0
  DamageFactor "PlayerSpellcard", 0.5
  +DONTHURTSPECIES
  +LOOKALLAROUND
  +FLOORCLIP
  +BOSS
  +NEVERRESPAWN
  +DONTMORPH
  +DONTRIP
  +NORADIUSDMG
  +AMBUSH
  +QUICKTORETALIATE
  +MISSILEMORE
  +MISSILEEVENMORE
  +NOICEDEATH
  MinMissileChance 160
  Painchance 1
  Seesound ""
  Painsound "touhou/pain"
  Deathsound "touhou/defeat" //never used
  Obituary "%o got in Reimu's way."
  DropItem "ReimuDancingYinYangOrbs"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    REIM A 0
	REIM A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,18,ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("BHI_SpellCardsBySkillLevel",6655),false)
	REIM A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,18,60)
  Idle:
	REIM BCDEFGHIJA 2 A_Look
	Loop
  See:
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("FLOAT",0)
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOGRAVITY",0)
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(32,"FastSee")
    REIM ABCDEFGHIJ 2 Fast A_Chase("Melee","Missile")
	REIM A 0 A_JumpIf(z-floorz > 96, "FastSee")
    Goto See+3
  FastSee:
	REIM L 0 ThrustThingZ(0,10,0,1)
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("FLOAT",1)
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOGRAVITY",1)
	REIM L 4 A_FaceTarget
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(32,"See")
	REIM MMNNOOPP 1 A_Chase("Melee2","AirMissile",CHF_FASTCHASE)
	REIM A 0 A_JumpIf(z-floorz < 32, "See")
    Goto FastSee+4
  Pain:
	REIM K 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0)
    REIM K 8 A_Pain //That's it.
    Goto See
  Melee:
	REI1 ABCD 3 Fast A_FaceTarget
	REI1 E 3 Fast A_CustomMeleeAttack(100,"touhou/remi/hit","none")
	REI1 FGHI 3 Fast A_FaceTarget
	Goto See
  Melee2:
    REI1 J 3 Fast A_FaceTarget
	REI1 K 3 Fast A_CustomMeleeAttack(50,"touhou/remi/hit","none")
	REI1 L 3 Fast A_FaceTarget
	Goto See
  Missile:
	REIM A 0 A_JumpIf(z-floorz > 64, "AirMissile")
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("FLOAT",0)
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOGRAVITY",0)
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(255,"SpreadAmulets1","SpreadAmulets1","SpreadAmulets2","SpreadAmulets2","HomingAmulet","YinYangOrb","Needles","YoukaiBuster")
	Goto SpreadAmulets1
  SpreadAmulets1:
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("EasyMode",1,"SpreadAmulets1Easy")
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("NormalMode",1,"SpreadAmulets1Normal")
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("HardMode",1,"SpreadAmulets1Hard")
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("LunaticMode",1,"SpreadAmulets1Lunatic")
	Goto SpreadAmulets1Hard
  SpreadAmulets1Easy:
	REI2 ABCD 3 A_FaceTarget
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,0)
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,10)
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,20)
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,30)
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,40)
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,50)
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,60)
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,70)
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,80)
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,90)
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,100)
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,110)
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,120)
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,130)
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,140)
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,150)
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,-10)
	REI2 E 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuSpreadAmulet1",32,0,-20)

	Goto See
  SpreadAmulets1Normal:
	REI2 ABCD 3 A_FaceTarget

	REI5 CDE 4 Fast A_FaceTarget
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(128,"AirMissile")
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(128,"Missile")
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(128,"FastSee")
	Goto See
  AirNeedles:
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("EasyMode",1,"AirNeedlesEasy")
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("NormalMode",1,"AirNeedlesNormal")
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("HardMode",1,"AirNeedlesHard")
	REMI A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("LunaticMode",1,"AirNeedlesLunatic")
	Goto AirNeedlesLunatic
  AirNeedlesEasy:
	REI5 IJK 6 A_FaceTarget
	REI5 L 6 A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,0,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REI5 M 0 A_FaceTarget
	REI5 M 6 A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,0,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REI5 N 0 A_FaceTarget
	REI5 N 6 A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,0,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(3,"AirMissile")
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(6,"See")
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(12,"Missile")
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(24,"FastSee")
	Goto AirNeedlesEasy+4
  AirNeedlesNormal:
	REI5 IJK 4 A_FaceTarget
	REI5 L 4 A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,0,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REI5 M 0 A_FaceTarget
	REI5 M 4 A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,0,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REI5 N 0 A_FaceTarget
	REI5 N 4 A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,0,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(3,"AirMissile")
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(6,"See")
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(12,"Missile")
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(24,"FastSee")
	Goto AirNeedlesNormal+4
  AirNeedlesHard:
	REI5 IJK 4 A_FaceTarget
	REI5 L 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,-4,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REI5 L 4 A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,4,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REI5 M 0 A_FaceTarget
	REI5 L 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,-4,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REI5 M 4 A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,4,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REI5 N 0 A_FaceTarget
	REI5 N 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,-4,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REI5 N 4 A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,4,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(3,"AirMissile")
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(6,"See")
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(12,"Missile")
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(24,"FastSee")
	Goto AirNeedlesHard+5
  AirNeedlesLunatic:
	REI5 IJK 3 Fast A_FaceTarget
	REI5 L 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,-4,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REI5 L 3 Fast A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,4,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REI5 M 0 A_FaceTarget
	REI5 M 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,-4,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REI5 M 3 Fast A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,4,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REI5 N 0 A_FaceTarget
	REI5 N 0 A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,-4,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REI5 N 3 Fast A_CustomMissile("ReimuPersuasionNeedle",32,4,0,CMF_AIMOFFSET)
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(3,"AirMissile")
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(6,"See")
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(12,"Missile")
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(24,"FastSee")
	Goto AirNeedlesLunatic+5
  Death:
	REIM K 1 ACS_NamedTerminate("BHI_BossStartAttack",0)
	REIM K 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStopAttack",0)
	REIM K 0 A_GiveInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1)
    REIM K 0 A_NoBlocking
	REIM K 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire")
	REIM KKKKKKKKK 2 A_FadeOut(0.1)
	Stop
  }
}
ACTOR ReimuSpreadAmulet1
{
  Radius 2
  Height 4
  Speed 20
  FastSpeed 30
  damage (12)
  Projectile
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  DamageType "ReimuDamage"
  //RenderStyle Add
  SeeSound "touhou/fire"
  DeathSound "touhou/hit"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    RAMU A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	Loop
  Death:
    RAMU AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR ReimuDancingYinYangOrbs : Reimu
{
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  DropItem "ReimuNS2"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    REIM A 0
	REIM A 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
	REIM ABCDEFGHIJ 3 A_FadeIn(0.1)
  Idle:
	REIM ABCDEFGHIJ 3 A_Look
	Goto Idle
  See:
	REI1 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0,0)
	REI1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"ChaseState")
    REI1 MNO 4 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6222)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6222,ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("BHI_SpellCardsBySkillLevel",6655),true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6222,60)
	REI1 A 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,91)
	REI1 A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	REI1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("SpellcardActive",1)
	REI1 PQRQRQRQRQRQR 3 A_FaceTarget
    REI1 STU 4 A_FaceTarget
	REI1 A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	REI1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
	Goto Missile
  ChaseState:
	REIM ABCDEFGHIJ 3 A_Chase
	Goto See
  Missile:
	REIM A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("EasyMode",1,"MissileEasy")
	REIM A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("NormalMode",1,"MissileNormal")
	REIM A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("HardMode",1,"MissileHard")
	REIM A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("LunaticMode",1,"MissileLunatic")
	Goto MissileHard

ACTOR ReimuDancingYinYangOrbsOrb1
{
  Projectile
  Radius 5
  Height 10
  Speed 30
  FastSpeed 45
  Damage (16)
  +BRIGHT
  -NOGRAVITY
  BounceType "Doom"
  Renderstyle Add
  Alpha 0.8
  Scale 0.8
  SeeSound "touhou/fire"
  BounceSound "touhou/hit2"
  DeathSound "touhou/hit"
  Decal BulletChip
  DamageType "ReimuDamage"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	RMYN EEEFFFGGGHHH 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
    Loop
  Death:
	RMYN EFGHEFGHEFGH 3 Bright A_FadeOut
    Loop
  }
}

    Loop

    Loop
  }
}

ACTOR ReimuNS2 : Reimu
{
  DropItem "ReimuFantasySealSpread"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    REIM A 0
	REIM A 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
	REIM ABCDEFGHIJ 3 A_FadeIn(0.1)
  Idle:
	REIM A 1 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6223)
	REIM A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6223,ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("BHI_SpellCardsBySkillLevel",5544),false)
	REIM A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6223,60)
	REIM BCDEFGHIJ 3 A_Look
	Goto Idle
  See:
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6223)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6223,ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("BHI_SpellCardsBySkillLevel",5544),false)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6223,60)
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("FLOAT",0)
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOGRAVITY",0)
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(32,"FastSee")
    REIM ABCDEFGHIJ 2 Fast A_Chase("Melee","Missile")
	REIM A 0 A_JumpIf(z-floorz > 96, "FastSee")
    Goto See+4
  FastSee:
	REIM L 0 ThrustThingZ(0,10,0,1)
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("FLOAT",1)
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOGRAVITY",1)
	REIM L 4 A_FaceTarget
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(32,"See")
	REIM MMNNOOPP 1 A_Chase("Melee2","AirMissile",CHF_FASTCHASE)
	REIM A 0 A_JumpIf(z-floorz < 32, "See")
    Goto FastSee+4
  }
}

ACTOR ReimuNS3 : Reimu
{
  DropItem "ReimuEvilSealingCircle"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    REIM A 0
	REIM A 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
	REIM ABCDEFGHIJ 3 A_FadeIn(0.1)
  Idle:
	REIM A 1 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6225)
	REIM A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6225,ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("BHI_SpellCardsBySkillLevel",4433),false)
	REIM A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6225,60)
	REIM BCDEFGHIJ 3 A_Look
	Goto Idle
  See:
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6225)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6225,ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("BHI_SpellCardsBySkillLevel",4433),false)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6225,60)
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("FLOAT",0)
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOGRAVITY",0)
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(32,"FastSee")
    REIM ABCDEFGHIJ 2 Fast A_Chase("Melee","Missile")
	REIM A 0 A_JumpIf(z-floorz > 96, "FastSee")
    Goto See+4
  FastSee:
	REIM L 0 ThrustThingZ(0,10,0,1)
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("FLOAT",1)
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOGRAVITY",1)
	REIM L 4 A_FaceTarget
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(32,"See")
	REIM MMNNOOPP 1 A_Chase("Melee2","AirMissile",CHF_FASTCHASE)

ACTOR ReimuEvilSealingCircleAttackEasy
{
  +NOINTERACTION
  +NOGRAVITY
  +OLDRADIUSDMG
  RenderStyle Add
  DamageType "ReimuDamage"
  var int user_count;
  var int user_dist;
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	TNT1 A 0
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetAngle(0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_dist",128)
	Goto SpawnCircle
  SpawnCircle:
	TNT1 A 1 A_JumpIf(user_count > 48, "PrepareToDie")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_count",user_count+1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailRed",user_dist,random(-user_dist,user_dist),random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailRed",-user_dist,random(-user_dist,user_dist),random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailRed",random(-user_dist,user_dist),user_dist,random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailRed",random(-user_dist,user_dist),-user_dist,random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailBlue",user_dist,random(-user_dist,user_dist),random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailBlue",-user_dist,random(-user_dist,user_dist),random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailBlue",random(-user_dist,user_dist),user_dist,random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailBlue",random(-user_dist,user_dist),-user_dist,random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailRed",user_dist,random(-user_dist,user_dist),random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailRed",-user_dist,random(-user_dist,user_dist),random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailRed",random(-user_dist,user_dist),user_dist,random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailRed",random(-user_dist,user_dist),-user_dist,random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailBlue",user_dist,random(-user_dist,user_dist),random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailBlue",-user_dist,random(-user_dist,user_dist),random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailBlue",random(-user_dist,user_dist),user_dist,random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailBlue",random(-user_dist,user_dist),-user_dist,random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailRed",user_dist,random(-user_dist,user_dist),random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailRed",-user_dist,random(-user_dist,user_dist),random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)

	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailRed",random(-user_dist,user_dist),-user_dist,random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)
	Loop
  PrepareToDie:
	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/reimu/seal",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	TNT1 A 0 A_Explode(200,user_dist,0,0,user_dist)
  DeathLoop:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_count > 1048, "Death")
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_count", user_count+1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("ReimuFantasySealOrbTrailRed",random(-user_dist,user_dist),random(-user_dist,user_dist),random(-z-floorz,ceilingz-z),0,0,4,0,0,0)

	Loop
  Death:
	TNT1 A 0
	Stop
  }
}

{
  DropItem "ReimuFantasySealConcentrate"

  {
  Spawn:
    REIM A 0
	REIM A 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
	REIM ABCDEFGHIJ 3 A_FadeIn(0.1)
  Idle:
	REIM A 1 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6227)
	REIM A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6227,ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("BHI_SpellCardsBySkillLevel",3322),false)
	REIM A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6227,60)
	REIM BCDEFGHIJ 3 A_Look
	Goto Idle
  See:
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6227)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6227,ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("BHI_SpellCardsBySkillLevel",3322),false)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6227,60)
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("FLOAT",0)
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOGRAVITY",0)
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(32,"FastSee")
    REIM ABCDEFGHIJ 2 Fast A_Chase("Melee","Missile")
	REIM A 0 A_JumpIf(z-floorz > 96, "FastSee")
    Goto See+4
  FastSee:
	REIM L 0 ThrustThingZ(0,10,0,1)
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("FLOAT",1)
	REIM L 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOGRAVITY",1)
	REIM L 4 A_FaceTarget
	REIM A 0 A_Jump(32,"See")
	REIM MMNNOOPP 1 A_Chase("Melee2","AirMissile",CHF_FASTCHASE)
	REIM A 0 A_JumpIf(z-floorz < 32, "See")
    Goto FastSee+4
  }
}

ACTOR ReimuFantasySealConcentrateAmulet
{
  Radius 2
  Height 4
  Speed 10
  FastSpeed 20
  damage (12)
  Projectile
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  DamageType "ReimuDamage"
  //RenderStyle Add
  SeeSound "touhou/fire"
  DeathSound "touhou/hit"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    WAMU A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	Loop
  Death:
    WAMU AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}

	FTS3 B 1 Bright A_SetScale(ScaleX+0.05)
	FTS3 B 1 Bright A_FadeOut(0.05)
	FTS3 B 1 Bright A_SetScale(ScaleX+0.05)
	FTS3 B 1 Bright A_FadeOut(0.05)
	FTS3 B 1 Bright A_SetScale(ScaleX+0.05)
	FTS3 B 1 Bright A_FadeOut(0.05)
	FTS3 B 1 Bright A_SetScale(ScaleX+0.05)
	Stop
  }
}

ACTOR ReimuDuplexBarrier : Reimu
{
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  DropItem "None"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    REIM A 0
	REIM A 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
	REIM ABCDEFGHIJ 3 A_FadeIn(0.1)
  Idle:
	REIM ABCDEFGHIJ 3 A_Look
	Goto Idle
  See:
	REI1 A 0 A_KillChildren
	REI1 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0,0)
	REI1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"ChaseState")
    REI1 MNO 4 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6229)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6229,ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("BHI_SpellCardsBySkillLevel",2211),true)

	REI1 A 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,95)
	REI1 A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)

	REI1 PQRQRQRQRQRQR 3 A_FaceTarget
    REI1 STU 4 A_FaceTarget
	REI1 A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	Goto Missile
  ChaseState:

ACTOR ReimuDuplexBarrierAmulet
{
  Radius 2
  Height 4
  Speed 12
  FastSpeed 12
  damage (12)
  Projectile
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  DamageType "ReimuDamage"
  //RenderStyle Add
  SeeSound "touhou/fire"
  DeathSound "touhou/hit"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	VAMU A 0
    VAMU AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	VAMU A 0 Bright A_Warp(AAPTR_TARGET,768,0,32,-1*angle,WARPF_ABSOLUTEANGLE|WARPF_USECALLERANGLE)
	VAMU A 0 Bright A_Stop
	VAMU A 0 Bright A_ChangeVelocity(12.0,0,0,CVF_RELATIVE)
  LoopState:
    VAMU A 1 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	Loop
  Death:
    VAMU AAAAAAAAAA 1 Bright A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR ReimuFantasySealBlink : Reimu
{
  -SOLID
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  +FLOAT
  +NOGRAVITY
  DropItem "None"
  DamageFactor "TouhouHakureiHomingAmulet", 0.6
  Health 1500
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    REIM A 0
	REIM A 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
	REIM ABCDEFGHIJ 3 A_FadeIn(0.1)
  Idle:
	REIM ABCDEFGHIJ 3 A_Look
	Goto Idle
  See:
	REI1 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0,0)
	REI1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"ChaseState")
    REI1 MNO 4 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6230)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6230,1,true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6230,110)
	REI1 A 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,96)
	REI1 A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	REI1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("SpellcardActive",1)
	REI1 PQRQRQRQRQRQR 3 A_FaceTarget
    REI1 STU 4 A_FaceTarget
	REI1 A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	REI1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
	Goto Missile
  ChaseState:
	REIM ABCDEFGHIJ 3 A_Chase
	Goto See
  Missile:
	REIM L 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("LunaticMode",1,"GottaGoFast")
	REIM LLLLLLLLLLLLLLLLLLLLLLLL 1 A_FaceTarget

ACTOR ReimuFlyingMysteriousShrineMaidenYinYangOrb
{
  +MISSILE
  +NOINTERACTION
  Scale 0.5

  var int user_warpangle;
  var int user_warpdist;

  States
  {
  Spawn:
    RMYN I 0
    RMYN I 0 Bright A_SetUserVar("user_warpangle", 0)
    RMYN I 0 Bright A_SetUserVar("user_warpdist", 2560)
	RMYN I 0 Bright A_Warp(AAPTR_TARGET, user_warpdist, 0, 32, user_warpangle, WARPF_ABSOLUTEANGLE|WARPF_NOCHECKPOSITION|WARPF_INTERPOLATE)
	RMYN I 0 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("TeleportFog",0,0,-16,0,0,0,0,0,0)
	Goto LoopState
  LoopState:
	RMYN I 0 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	RMYN I 0 Bright A_JumpIf(user_warpdist <= 32, "LoopState2")
	RMYN I 0 Bright A_FaceTarget
	RMYN I 0 Bright A_SetAngle(angle+180)
	RMYN I 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("ReimuFlyingMysteriousShrineMaidenAmulet0",0,0,0,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
    RMYN I 0 Bright A_SetUserVar("user_warpdist", user_warpdist-4)
    RMYN I 0 Bright A_SetUserVar("user_warpangle", user_warpangle+1)
	RMYN I 3 Bright A_Warp(AAPTR_TARGET, user_warpdist, 0, 32, user_warpangle, WARPF_ABSOLUTEANGLE|WARPF_NOCHECKPOSITION|WARPF_INTERPOLATE)
	Loop
  LoopState2:
	RMYN I 0 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Death")
	RMYN I 0 Bright A_FaceTarget
	RMYN I 0 Bright A_SetAngle(angle+180)
	RMYN I 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("ReimuFlyingMysteriousShrineMaidenAmulet0",0,0,0,CMF_AIMDIRECTION)
    RMYN I 0 Bright A_SetUserVar("user_warpangle", user_warpangle+1)
	RMYN I 3 Bright A_Warp(AAPTR_TARGET, 32, 0, 32, user_warpangle, WARPF_ABSOLUTEANGLE|WARPF_NOCHECKPOSITION|WARPF_INTERPOLATE)
	Loop
  Death:
    RMYN IIIIIIIIII 5 A_FadeOut
    Stop
  }
}

ACTOR ReimuFantasyHeaven : Reimu
{
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    REIM A 0
	REIM A 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
	REIM ABCDEFGHIJ 3 A_FadeIn(0.1)
  Idle:
	REIM ABCDEFGHIJ 3 A_Look
	Goto Idle
  See:
	REI1 A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0,0)
    REI1 MNO 4 A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartSurvivalAttack",0,0)
	REI1 A 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,98)
	REI1 A 0 ACS_Execute(61,0)
	REI1 A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	REI1 PQRQRQRQRQRQRQRQRQRQRQRQRQR 3 A_FaceTarget
    REI1 STU 4 A_FaceTarget
	REI1 A 0 A_Die
  Death:
  XDeath:
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedTerminate("BHI_BossStartSurvivalAttack",0)
	REIM K 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStopAttack",0)
	REI1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("TeleportFog",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,0,0)
	Stop
  }
}
